# TOPBAR  (shared component for both pages)
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
def render_topbar(page_label: str) -> None:
    """Injects sticky top nav. page_label is shown as breadcrumb."""
    ui.add_head_html(HEAD_HTML)
    ui.add_body_html(
        f'<div class="topbar">'
        f'  <div class="topbar-left">'
        f"    <div>"
        f'      <div class="topbar-brand">🚗 AutoAudit MIS</div>'
        f'      <div class="topbar-sub">Automobile Sales Audit System</div>'
        f"    </div>"
        f'    <div class="topbar-divider"></div>'
        f'    <div class="topbar-breadcrumb"><b>{page_label}</b></div>'
        f"  </div>"
        f'  <div style="background:#E8402A;color:#fff;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;'
        f'       letter-spacing:.6px;padding:3px 10px;border-radius:20px;">AUDIT PORTAL</div>'
        f"</div>"
    )


# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# MIS TABLE RENDERING & HELPER METHODS
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
def build_ordered_columns(row: dict):
    """
    Build ordered columns for the MIS table.
    """
    keys = list(row.keys())

    def pick(prefix):
        return [k for k in keys if k.startswith(prefix)]

    #  GROUPS (based on your backend naming)
    ordered = []

    # 1. Core info
    ordered += [
        "id",
        "customer_name",
        "mobile_number",
        "variant_name",
        "booking_date",
    ]

    # 2. Price components
    ordered += pick("Ex ") + pick("Insurance") + pick("Registration")

    # 3. Discount components
    ordered += [k for k in keys if "_actual" in k and "Discount" in k]

    # 4. Allowed + diff (keep near actual)
    ordered += [k for k in keys if "_allowed" in k]
    ordered += [k for k in keys if "_diff" in k]

    # 5. Conditions
    ordered += pick("cond_")

    # 6. Accessories / finance / exchange
    ordered += pick("accessories_")
    ordered += pick("finance_")
    ordered += pick("exchange_")

    # 7. Checklist
    ordered += pick("checklist_")

    # 8. Audit
    ordered += pick("audit_")

    # 9. Totals
    ordered += [
        "total_actual_discount",
        "total_allowed_discount",
        "total_excess_discount",
        "status",
    ]

    # remove duplicates + preserve order
    seen = set()
    ordered = [x for x in ordered if not (x in seen or seen.add(x))]

    return ordered


def clear_label(column_name: str):
    """
    Cleans up column names for display.
    """
    return (
        column_name.replace("_", " ")
        .replace("actual", "(Actual)")
        .replace("allowed", "(Allowed)")
        .replace("diff", "(Diff)")
        .title()
    )


def render_table(transactions):
    """
    Renders the MIS transaction table with:
    - Inter font (readable, not monospace) for text cells
    - JetBrains Mono only for numeric/amount columns
    - Global search bar
    - Per-column filter inputs
    - Status-based row colouring
    - Click-to-edit navigation
    """
    if not transactions:
        ui.html("""
            <div style="text-align:center;padding:64px 0;color:#9CA3AF;">
              <div style="font-size:36px;margin-bottom:10px">📭</div>
              <div style="font-size:14px;font-weight:500;color:#6B7280">No transactions yet</div>
              <div style="font-size:12px;margin-top:4px">Click "New Entry" to add the first record.</div>
            </div>
        """)
        return

    ordered_keys = build_ordered_columns(transactions[0])

    # Mark numeric columns so we can apply mono font in the slot
    MONO_COLS = {
        k
        for k in ordered_keys
        if any(
            t in k
            for t in (
                "_actual",
                "_allowed",
                "_diff",
                "total_",
                "price",
                "amount",
                "discount",
                "excess",
                "id",
                "payment",
                "invoice_",
            )
        )
    }
    STATUS_COL = "status"

    cols = [
        {
            "name": key,
            "label": clear_label(key),
            "field": key,
            "align": "right" if key in MONO_COLS else "left",
            "sortable": True,
        }
        for key in ordered_keys
    ]

    # ── Toolbar: search + column-filter toggles ──────────────
    with ui.element("div").classes("table-toolbar"):
        # Global search
        with ui.element("div").classes("search-wrap"):
            ui.html('<span class="search-icon">🔍</span>')
            search_input = (
                ui.input(placeholder="Search all columns…")
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense clearable")
                .style("font-size:13px")
            )

        ui.html(
            '<span style="font-size:11px;color:#9CA3AF;padding:0 4px">Filters:</span>'
        )

        # Status filter
        status_vals = sorted(
            {str(t.get("status", "")) for t in transactions if t.get("status")}
        )
        status_filter = (
            ui.select(
                options={"": "All Status"} | {v: v for v in status_vals},
                value="",
                label="Status",
            )
            .classes("w-32")
            .props("outlined dense")
        )

        # Variant filter
        variant_vals = sorted(
            {
                str(t.get("variant_name", ""))
                for t in transactions
                if t.get("variant_name")
            }
        )
        variant_filter = (
            ui.select(
                options={"": "All Variants"} | {v: v for v in variant_vals},
                value="",
                label="Variant",
            )
            .classes("w-40")
            .props("outlined dense")
        )

        ui.space()
        ui.html(
            f'<span style="font-size:11px;color:#9CA3AF">{len(transactions)} records</span>'
        )

    # ── Table ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
    with ui.element("div").style("overflow-x:auto;width:100%;"):
        table = (
            ui.table(
                columns=cols,
                rows=transactions,
                row_key="id",
            )
            .classes("w-full mis-tbl")
            .props("flat dense separator=cell virtual-scroll")
            .style("min-height:300px; max-height:calc(100vh - 320px);")
        )

    # ── Row rendering slot (font + colouring + click) ─────────
    mono_set_js = "[" + ",".join(f'"{k}"' for k in MONO_COLS) + "]"
    table.add_slot(
        "body",
        f"""
        <q-tr :props="props"
              :class="props.row.status === 'Excess' ? 'row-excess' : ''"
              @click="$parent.$emit('row-click', props.row)"
              style="cursor:pointer">
          <q-td v-for="col in props.cols" :key="col.name" :props="props"
                :class="{mono_set_js}.includes(col.name) ? 'mono' : ''">
            <template v-if="col.name === 'status'">
              <span :class="props.row.status === 'Excess' ? 'pill pill-excess' : 'pill pill-ok'">
                {{ col.value }}
              </span>
            </template>
            <template v-else-if="col.name === 'id'">
              <span style="color:#9CA3AF;font-family:\'JetBrains Mono\',monospace;font-size:11px">#{{ col.value }}</span>
            </template>
            <template v-else>{{ col.value }}</template>
          </q-td>
        </q-tr>
    """,
    )

    # Empty state
    table.add_slot(
        "no-data",
        """
        <div style="text-align:center;padding:48px 0;color:#9CA3AF;">
          <div style="font-size:24px;margin-bottom:8px">🔍</div>
          <div style="font-size:13px">No records match your filters.</div>
        </div>
    """,
    )

    # ── Wire up search + filters (client-side via binding) ────
    table.on(
        "row-click",
        lambda e: ui.navigate.to(f"/form?transaction_id={e.args.get('id')}"),
    )

    def apply_filters():
        q = (search_input.value or "").strip().lower()
        sf = (status_filter.value or "").strip()
        vf = (variant_filter.value or "").strip()
        filtered = []
        for row in transactions:
            if sf and str(row.get("status", "")) != sf:
                continue
            if vf and str(row.get("variant_name", "")) != vf:
                continue
            if q:
                haystack = " ".join(str(v) for v in row.values()).lower()
                if q not in haystack:
                    continue
            filtered.append(row)
        table.rows = filtered

    search_input.on("update:model-value", lambda _: apply_filters())
    status_filter.on("update:model-value", lambda _: apply_filters())
    variant_filter.on("update:model-value", lambda _: apply_filters())


# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
#          SVG LINE CHART HELPER
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
def _svg_line_chart(
    series: list[tuple[str, list]],  # [(label, [values...]), ...]
    x_labels: list[str],
    colors: list[str],
    width: int = 520,
    height: int = 160,
    y_suffix: str = "K",
    title: str = "",
) -> str:
    """
    Renders a clean SVG line chart with:
    - Multiple series support
    - Smooth polyline paths
    - Dotted gridlines
    - Axis labels
    - Interactive hover tooltips via title elements
    - Legend
    """
    pad_left, pad_right, pad_top, pad_bottom = 52, 16, 18, 36
    cw = width - pad_left - pad_right
    ch = height - pad_top - pad_bottom

    # Flatten all values to get global max
    all_vals = [v for _, vals in series for v in vals]
    y_max = max(all_vals) if all_vals else 1
    y_max = y_max or 1  # guard zero

    n = len(x_labels)
    if n < 2:
        return f'<div style="color:#9CA3AF;font-size:12px;padding:20px 0;text-align:center">Not enough data points</div>'

    def x_pos(i):
        return pad_left + (i / (n - 1)) * cw

    def y_pos(v):
        return pad_top + ch - (v / y_max) * ch

    # Grid lines (5 horizontal)
    grid_lines = ""
    for k in range(5):
        y_val = y_max * k / 4
        yp = y_pos(y_val)
        label_v = f"{y_val / 1000:.0f}K" if y_suffix == "K" else f"{y_val:.0f}"
        grid_lines += (
            f'<line x1="{pad_left}" y1="{yp:.1f}" x2="{width - pad_right}" y2="{yp:.1f}" '
            f'stroke="#F0F1F5" stroke-width="1" stroke-dasharray="3,3"/>'
            f'<text x="{pad_left - 6}" y="{yp + 4:.1f}" text-anchor="end" '
            f'font-size="9" fill="#9CA3AF" font-family="JetBrains Mono,monospace">{label_v}</text>'
        )

    # X axis labels
    x_axis = ""
    step = max(1, n // 6)
    for i, lbl in enumerate(x_labels):
        if i % step == 0 or i == n - 1:
            xp = x_pos(i)
            x_axis += (
                f'<text x="{xp:.1f}" y="{height - 6}" text-anchor="middle" '
                f'font-size="9" fill="#9CA3AF" font-family="Inter,sans-serif">{lbl}</text>'
            )

    # Series paths + dots
    series_svg = ""
    for idx, (s_label, vals) in enumerate(series):
        col = colors[idx % len(colors)]
        points = [(x_pos(i), y_pos(v)) for i, v in enumerate(vals)]
        poly = " ".join(f"{x:.1f},{y:.1f}" for x, y in points)
        series_svg += (
            f'<polyline points="{poly}" fill="none" stroke="{col}" '
            f'stroke-width="2" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-linecap="round"/>'
        )
        # Gradient fill under line
        fill_pts = (
            f"{points[0][0]:.1f},{pad_top + ch} "
            + poly
            + f" {points[-1][0]:.1f},{pad_top + ch}"
        )
        series_svg += f'<polygon points="{fill_pts}" fill="{col}" opacity="0.07"/>'
        # Dots + tooltip
        for i, (xp, yp) in enumerate(points):
            raw = vals[i]
            tip = (
                f"{x_labels[i]}: ₹{raw / 1000:.1f}K"
                if y_suffix == "K"
                else f"{x_labels[i]}: {raw}"
            )
            series_svg += (
                f'<circle cx="{xp:.1f}" cy="{yp:.1f}" r="3" fill="{col}" stroke="#fff" stroke-width="1.5">'
                f"<title>{tip}</title></circle>"
            )

    # Legend
    legend_svg = ""
    lx = pad_left
    for idx, (s_label, _) in enumerate(series):
        col = colors[idx % len(colors)]
        legend_svg += (
            f'<rect x="{lx}" y="4" width="10" height="4" rx="2" fill="{col}"/>'
            f'<text x="{lx + 13}" y="10" font-size="9" fill="#6B7280" font-family="Inter,sans-serif">{s_label}</text>'
        )
        lx += len(s_label) * 5.5 + 24

    return (
        f'<svg viewBox="0 0 {width} {height}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" '
        f'style="width:100%;height:{height}px;overflow:visible">'
        f"{grid_lines}{x_axis}{series_svg}{legend_svg}"
        f"</svg>"
    )


# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
#          HORIZONTAL BAR CHART HELPER (reusable)
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
def _bar_chart_html(
    items: list[tuple[str, float]],  # [(label, value), ...]
    color: str = "#6366F1",
    value_fmt: str = "K",  # "K" → ₹XK, "N" → integer count, "raw" → ₹X,000
    max_items: int = 8,
    empty_msg: str = "No data yet",
) -> str:
    if not items:
        return f'<div style="color:#9CA3AF;font-size:12px;padding:20px 0;text-align:center">{empty_msg}</div>'
    top = items[:max_items]
    max_val = max(v for _, v in top) or 1

    def fmt(v):
        if value_fmt == "K":
            return f"₹{v / 1000:.1f}K"
        elif value_fmt == "raw":
            return f"₹{v:,.0f}"
        else:
            return f"{int(v)}"

    rows = ""
    for lbl, val in top:
        pct = int(val / max_val * 100)
        rows += f"""
        <div class="bar-row">
          <div class="bar-label" title="{lbl}">{lbl}</div>
          <div class="bar-track">
            <div class="bar-fill" style="width:{pct}%;background:{color}"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="bar-val">{fmt(val)}</div>
        </div>"""
    return rows


# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
#                        PAGE 1: DASHBOARD
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
@ui.page("/")
async def dashboard_page() -> None:
    render_topbar("Dashboard")

    # ── Fetch transactions ─────────────────────────────────
    try:
        transactions: list = await api_get("/transactions")
    except Exception:
        transactions = []

    # ── Core aggregates ────────────────────────────────────
    from collections import defaultdict
    import calendar

    total_entries = len(transactions)
    total_discount = sum(t.get("total_allowed_discount", 0) or 0 for t in transactions)
    total_excess = sum(t.get("total_excess_discount", 0) or 0 for t in transactions)
    excess_cases = sum(1 for t in transactions if t.get("status") == "Excess")
    ok_cases = total_entries - excess_cases
    compliance_pct = round(
        (ok_cases / total_entries * 100) if total_entries else 100, 1
    )
    avg_discount = round(total_discount / total_entries) if total_entries else 0

    # ── Month helpers ──────────────────────────────────────
    def month_label(ym: str) -> str:
        try:
            y, m = ym.split("-")
            return f"{calendar.month_abbr[int(m)]} '{y[2:]}"
        except Exception:
            return ym

    month_map: dict = defaultdict(list)
    for t in transactions:
        bd = t.get("booking_date", "")
        if bd and len(bd) >= 7:
            month_map[bd[:7]].append(t)
    sorted_months = sorted(month_map.keys(), reverse=True)

    # ── TIME SERIES DATA (line chart — all months, chronological) ──
    chrono_months = sorted(month_map.keys())  # oldest → newest
    ts_labels = [month_label(ym) for ym in chrono_months]
    ts_discount = [
        sum(t.get("total_allowed_discount", 0) or 0 for t in month_map[ym])
        for ym in chrono_months
    ]
    ts_excess = [
        sum(t.get("total_excess_discount", 0) or 0 for t in month_map[ym])
        for ym in chrono_months
    ]
    ts_count = [len(month_map[ym]) for ym in chrono_months]

    # ── SALES ANALYTICS ───────────────────────────────────
    # Sales by car model (count of transactions per model)
    model_sales: dict = defaultdict(int)
    model_discount: dict = defaultdict(int)
    for t in transactions:
        model = (
            t.get("car_name")
            or t.get("car")
            or (
                t.get("variant_name", "").split(" ")[0]
                if t.get("variant_name")
                else "Unknown"
            )
        )
        model_sales[model] += 1
        model_discount[model] += t.get("total_allowed_discount", 0) or 0

    top_model_sales = sorted(model_sales.items(), key=lambda x: -x[1])[:8]
    top_model_disc = sorted(model_discount.items(), key=lambda x: -x[1])[:8]

    # Sales by condition (exchange, corporate, etc.)
    condition_counts: dict = defaultdict(int)
    for t in transactions:
        conds = t.get("conditions", {}) or {}
        for k, v in conds.items():
            if v:
                condition_counts[k.replace("_", " ").title()] += 1

    # ── VARIANT-WISE EXCESS ────────────────────────────────
    variant_excess: dict = defaultdict(int)
    for t in transactions:
        vname = t.get("variant_name") or t.get("variant") or "Unknown"
        ex = t.get("total_excess_discount", 0) or 0
        if ex > 0:
            variant_excess[vname] += ex
    top_variants = sorted(variant_excess.items(), key=lambda x: -x[1])[:8]

    # ── CAR MODEL EXCESS ──────────────────────────────────
    model_excess: dict = defaultdict(int)
    for t in transactions:
        model = (
            t.get("car_name")
            or t.get("car")
            or (
                t.get("variant_name", "").split(" ")[0]
                if t.get("variant_name")
                else "Unknown"
            )
        )
        ex = t.get("total_excess_discount", 0) or 0
        if ex > 0:
            model_excess[model] += ex
    top_model_excess = sorted(model_excess.items(), key=lambda x: -x[1])[:8]

    # ── OUTLET-WISE ANALYTICS ─────────────────────────────
    outlet_sales: dict = defaultdict(int)
    outlet_discount: dict = defaultdict(int)
    outlet_excess: dict = defaultdict(int)
    for t in transactions:
        outlet = t.get("outlet_name") or t.get("outlet") or "Unknown"
        outlet_sales[outlet] += 1
        outlet_discount[outlet] += t.get("total_allowed_discount", 0) or 0
        outlet_excess[outlet] += t.get("total_excess_discount", 0) or 0

    outlets_sorted_sales = sorted(outlet_sales.items(), key=lambda x: -x[1])[:8]
    outlets_sorted_disc = sorted(outlet_discount.items(), key=lambda x: -x[1])[:8]

    # ── TOP EXCESS CUSTOMERS ──────────────────────────────
    top_excess_txns = sorted(
        [t for t in transactions if (t.get("total_excess_discount", 0) or 0) > 0],
        key=lambda x: -(x.get("total_excess_discount", 0) or 0),
    )[:6]

    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    # LAYOUT: sidebar (left) + main content (right)
    # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    with ui.element("div").classes("dash-layout"):
        # ── SIDEBAR ─────────────────────────────────────────
        with ui.element("div").classes("dash-sidebar"):
            ui.html('<div class="sidebar-section-label">Quick Nav</div>')
            ui.html("""
                <a href="/" class="sidebar-month-item active">📊 &nbsp;Dashboard</a>
                <a href="/mis-table" class="sidebar-month-item">📋 &nbsp;MIS Table</a>
            """)
            ui.html('<div class="sidebar-divider"></div>')
            ui.html('<div class="sidebar-section-label">Month-wise MIS</div>')
            if sorted_months:
                for ym in sorted_months:
                    txns_in_month = month_map[ym]
                    cnt = len(txns_in_month)
                    exc = sum(1 for t in txns_in_month if t.get("status") == "Excess")
                    lbl = month_label(ym)
                    badge_extra = (
                        f' style="background:#FECDC8;color:#C0392B"' if exc > 0 else ""
                    )
                    ui.html(
                        f'<a href="/mis-table?month={ym}" class="sidebar-month-item">'
                        f"  {lbl}"
                        f'  <span class="sidebar-month-badge"{badge_extra}>{cnt}</span>'
                        f"</a>"
                    )
            else:
                ui.html(
                    '<div style="padding:8px 18px;font-size:12px;color:#9CA3AF">No data yet</div>'
                )
            ui.html('<div class="sidebar-divider"></div>')
            ui.html('<div class="sidebar-section-label">Quick Actions</div>')
            ui.html("""
                <a href="/form" class="sidebar-month-item">➕ &nbsp;New Entry</a>
                <a href="/settings" class="sidebar-month-item">⚙️ &nbsp;Settings</a>
            """)

        # ── MAIN CONTENT ─────────────────────────────────────
        with ui.element("div").classes("dash-main"):
            # ── Page header ──────────────────────────────────
            with ui.element("div").classes("section-header"):
                with ui.element("div"):
                    ui.html('<div class="section-title-text">Dashboard</div>')
                    ui.html(
                        '<div class="section-subtitle">Overview of all audit transactions</div>'
                    )
                ui.button(
                    "➕  New Entry", on_click=lambda: ui.navigate.to("/form")
                ).classes("btn-add").props("no-caps unelevated")

            # ════════════════════════════════════════════════
            # ROW 1 — KPI CARDS
            # ════════════════════════════════════════════════
            excess_color = "#EF4444" if total_excess > 0 else "#10B981"
            compliance_color = (
                "#10B981"
                if compliance_pct >= 80
                else "#F59E0B"
                if compliance_pct >= 60
                else "#EF4444"
            )
            ui.html(f"""
            <div class="kpi-grid">
              <div class="kpi-card" style="--kpi-color:#6366F1">
                <div class="kpi-icon">📋</div>
                <div class="kpi-label">Total Transactions</div>
                <div class="kpi-value">{total_entries}</div>
                <div class="kpi-sub">
                  <span style="color:#6366F1">{ok_cases} Under Limit</span>&nbsp;·&nbsp;
                  <span style="color:#EF4444">{excess_cases} Excess</span>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div class="kpi-card" style="--kpi-color:#10B981">
                <div class="kpi-icon">💸</div>
                <div class="kpi-label">Total Allowed Discount</div>
                <div class="kpi-value accent">₹{total_discount:,.0f}</div>
                <div class="kpi-sub">Avg ₹{avg_discount:,.0f} per transaction</div>
              </div>
              <div class="kpi-card" style="--kpi-color:{excess_color}">
                <div class="kpi-icon">⚠️</div>
                <div class="kpi-label">Total Excess Discount</div>
                <div class="kpi-value" style="color:{excess_color}">₹{total_excess:,.0f}</div>
                <div class="kpi-sub">
                  {'<span class="down">Requires attention</span>' if total_excess > 0 else '<span class="up">All within limits</span>'}
                </div>
              </div>
              <div class="kpi-card" style="--kpi-color:{compliance_color}">
                <div class="kpi-icon">✅</div>
                <div class="kpi-label">Compliance Rate</div>
                <div class="kpi-value" style="color:{compliance_color}">{compliance_pct}%</div>
                <div class="kpi-sub">{ok_cases} of {total_entries} transactions OK</div>
              </div>
            </div>
            """)

            # ════════════════════════════════════════════════
            # ROW 2 — TIME SERIES LINE CHART (full width)
            # ════════════════════════════════════════════════
            with ui.element("div").classes("dash-panel").style("margin-bottom:14px"):
                ui.html(
                    '<div class="dash-panel-title">Discount &amp; Excess Trend '
                    "<span>month-on-month, all time</span></div>"
                )
                if len(chrono_months) >= 2:
                    chart_svg = _svg_line_chart(
                        series=[
                            ("Allowed Discount", ts_discount),
                            ("Excess Discount", ts_excess),
                        ],
                        x_labels=ts_labels,
                        colors=["#6366F1", "#EF4444"],
                        width=880,
                        height=180,
                        y_suffix="K",
                    )
                    ui.html(chart_svg)
                    # Mini stats below chart
                    peak_month = (
                        ts_labels[ts_discount.index(max(ts_discount))]
                        if ts_discount
                        else "—"
                    )
                    worst_month = (
                        ts_labels[ts_excess.index(max(ts_excess))] if ts_excess else "—"
                    )
                    ui.html(f"""
                    <div style="display:flex;gap:24px;margin-top:10px;padding-top:10px;
                                border-top:1px solid #F3F4F6;flex-wrap:wrap">
                      <div style="font-size:11px;color:#6B7280">
                        Peak discount month: <b style="color:#6366F1">{peak_month}</b>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-size:11px;color:#6B7280">
                        Highest excess month: <b style="color:#EF4444">{worst_month}</b>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-size:11px;color:#6B7280">
                        Total months tracked: <b style="color:#374151">{len(chrono_months)}</b>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    """)
                else:
                    # Fallback — also show transaction count line if only 1 month
                    ui.html(
                        '<div style="color:#9CA3AF;font-size:12px;padding:28px 0;text-align:center">'
                        "At least 2 months of data needed for the trend chart.</div>"
                    )

            # ════════════════════════════════════════════════
            # ROW 3 — SALES ANALYTICS  (2-col)
            # ════════════════════════════════════════════════
            ui.html(
                '<div class="dash-panel-title" style="margin:4px 0 10px;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:#111827">Sales Analytics</div>'
            )
            with ui.element("div").classes("dash-row2"):
                # Panel A — Sales count by car model
                with ui.element("div").classes("dash-panel"):
                    ui.html(
                        '<div class="dash-panel-title">Units Sold by Car Model <span>all time</span></div>'
                    )
                    ui.html(
                        _bar_chart_html(
                            top_model_sales,
                            color="#6366F1",
                            value_fmt="N",
                            empty_msg="No model data available",
                        )
                    )

                # Panel B — Discount by car model
                with ui.element("div").classes("dash-panel"):
                    ui.html(
                        '<div class="dash-panel-title">Discount by Car Model <span>total allowed</span></div>'
                    )
                    ui.html(
                        _bar_chart_html(
                            top_model_disc,
                            color="#10B981",
                            value_fmt="K",
                            empty_msg="No model data available",
                        )
                    )

            # Sale conditions breakdown (full-width compact)
            if condition_counts:
                sorted_conds = sorted(condition_counts.items(), key=lambda x: -x[1])
                max_cond = max(v for _, v in sorted_conds) or 1
                cond_bars = ""
                for lbl, cnt in sorted_conds:
                    pct = int(cnt / max_cond * 100)
                    cond_bars += f"""
                    <div class="bar-row">
                      <div class="bar-label">{lbl}</div>
                      <div class="bar-track">
                        <div class="bar-fill" style="width:{pct}%;background:#8B5CF6"></div>
                      </div>
                      <div class="bar-val">{cnt} txns</div>
                    </div>"""
                with (
                    ui.element("div").classes("dash-panel").style("margin-bottom:14px")
                ):
                    ui.html(
                        '<div class="dash-panel-title">Sales Conditions Breakdown <span>how many transactions had each flag</span></div>'
                    )
                    cols_per_row = 2
                    items_list = list(sorted_conds)
                    half = (len(items_list) + 1) // 2
                    left_items = items_list[:half]
                    right_items = items_list[half:]
                    left_html = _bar_chart_html(
                        left_items, color="#8B5CF6", value_fmt="N"
                    )
                    right_html = _bar_chart_html(
                        right_items, color="#8B5CF6", value_fmt="N"
                    )
                    ui.html(f"""
                    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:16px">
                      <div>{left_html}</div>
                      <div>{right_html}</div>
                    </div>
                    """)

            # ════════════════════════════════════════════════
            # ROW 4 — OUTLET-WISE ANALYTICS  (2-col)
            # ════════════════════════════════════════════════
            ui.html(
                '<div class="dash-panel-title" style="margin:4px 0 10px;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:#111827">Outlet Analytics</div>'
            )
            with ui.element("div").classes("dash-row2"):
                # Panel C — Outlet sales count
                with ui.element("div").classes("dash-panel"):
                    ui.html(
                        '<div class="dash-panel-title">Sales by Outlet <span>transaction count</span></div>'
                    )
                    ui.html(
                        _bar_chart_html(
                            outlets_sorted_sales,
                            color="#0EA5E9",
                            value_fmt="N",
                            empty_msg="No outlet data — check outlet_name field in API",
                        )
                    )

                # Panel D — Outlet discount
                with ui.element("div").classes("dash-panel"):
                    ui.html(
                        '<div class="dash-panel-title">Discount by Outlet <span>total allowed</span></div>'
                    )
                    ui.html(
                        _bar_chart_html(
                            outlets_sorted_disc,
                            color="#F59E0B",
                            value_fmt="K",
                            empty_msg="No outlet data — check outlet_name field in API",
                        )
                    )

            # Outlet excess table (full width compact)
            if outlet_excess:
                sorted_outlets = sorted(outlet_excess.items(), key=lambda x: -x[1])
                max_oe = max(v for _, v in sorted_outlets) or 1
                with (
                    ui.element("div").classes("dash-panel").style("margin-bottom:14px")
                ):
                    ui.html(
                        '<div class="dash-panel-title">Excess Discount by Outlet <span>problem outlets</span></div>'
                    )
                    rows_html = ""
                    for o_name, o_exc in sorted_outlets[:8]:
                        pct = int(o_exc / max_oe * 100)
                        sales = outlet_sales.get(o_name, 0)
                        disc = outlet_discount.get(o_name, 0)
                        exc_rt = round(o_exc / disc * 100, 1) if disc else 0
                        rows_html += f"""
                        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:140px 1fr 90px 80px 70px;
                                    gap:8px;align-items:center;padding:7px 0;
                                    border-bottom:1px solid #F9FAFB;font-size:12px;">
                          <span style="font-weight:500;color:#374151;
                                       overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap"
                                title="{o_name}">{o_name}</span>
                          <div class="bar-track">
                            <div class="bar-fill" style="width:{pct}%;background:#EF4444"></div>
                          </div>
                          <span style="font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;color:#DC2626;
                                       font-weight:600;text-align:right">₹{o_exc / 1000:.1f}K</span>
                          <span style="font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;color:#6B7280;
                                       text-align:right">{sales} sales</span>
                          <span style="color:{"#DC2626" if exc_rt > 20 else "#9CA3AF"};
                                       text-align:right;font-size:11px">{exc_rt}%</span>
                        </div>"""
                    ui.html(f"""
                    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:140px 1fr 90px 80px 70px;
                                gap:8px;font-size:9.5px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:.6px;
                                text-transform:uppercase;color:#9CA3AF;padding-bottom:6px;
                                border-bottom:2px solid #F0F1F5">
                      <span>Outlet</span><span></span>
                      <span style="text-align:right">Excess</span>
                      <span style="text-align:right">Sales</span>
                      <span style="text-align:right">Exc%</span>
                    </div>
                    {rows_html}
                    """)

            # ════════════════════════════════════════════════
            # ROW 5 — EXCESS ANALYSIS  (2-col: model + variant)
            # ════════════════════════════════════════════════
            ui.html(
                '<div class="dash-panel-title" style="margin:4px 0 10px;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:#111827">Excess Discount Analysis</div>'
            )
            with ui.element("div").classes("dash-row2"):
                # Panel E — Excess by Car Model
                with ui.element("div").classes("dash-panel"):
                    ui.html(
                        '<div class="dash-panel-title">Excess by Car Model <span>aggregated</span></div>'
                    )
                    ui.html(
                        _bar_chart_html(
                            top_model_excess,
                            color="#F97316",
                            value_fmt="K",
                            empty_msg="No excess discounts by model 🎉",
                        )
                    )

                # Panel F — Excess by Variant
                with ui.element("div").classes("dash-panel"):
                    ui.html(
                        '<div class="dash-panel-title">Excess by Variant <span>granular view</span></div>'
                    )
                    ui.html(
                        _bar_chart_html(
                            top_variants,
                            color="#EF4444",
                            value_fmt="K",
                            empty_msg="No excess discounts 🎉",
                        )
                    )

            # ════════════════════════════════════════════════
            # ROW 6 — TOP EXCESS TXNS + MONTH SUMMARY
            # ════════════════════════════════════════════════
            with ui.element("div").classes("dash-row2"):
                # Panel G: Top excess customers
                with ui.element("div").classes("dash-panel"):
                    ui.html(
                        '<div class="dash-panel-title">Top Excess Transactions <span>by amount</span></div>'
                    )
                    if top_excess_txns:
                        for t in top_excess_txns:
                            name = t.get("customer_name") or t.get("customer") or "—"
                            ex = t.get("total_excess_discount", 0) or 0
                            var = t.get("variant_name") or t.get("variant") or "—"
                            txid = t.get("id", "")
                            bd = t.get("booking_date", "—")
                            ui.html(f"""
                            <div class="excess-row"
                                 onclick="location.href='/form?transaction_id={txid}'"
                                 style="cursor:pointer">
                              <div>
                                <div class="excess-name">{name}</div>
                                <div class="excess-tag">{var} &middot; {bd}</div>
                              </div>
                              <div class="excess-val">₹{ex:,.0f}</div>
                            </div>
                            """)
                    else:
                        ui.html(
                            '<div style="color:#9CA3AF;font-size:12px;padding:20px 0;text-align:center">No excess transactions 🎉</div>'
                        )

                # Panel H: Month-wise summary table
                with ui.element("div").classes("dash-panel"):
                    ui.html(
                        '<div class="dash-panel-title">Month-wise Summary <span>all months</span></div>'
                    )
                    if sorted_months:
                        ui.html("""
                        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 50px 70px 70px;
                                    gap:0;font-size:9.5px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:.6px;
                                    text-transform:uppercase;color:#9CA3AF;
                                    padding:0 0 6px;border-bottom:1px solid #F3F4F6;margin-bottom:4px">
                          <span>Month</span>
                          <span style="text-align:right">Txns</span>
                          <span style="text-align:right">Disc</span>
                          <span style="text-align:right">Excess</span>
                        </div>
                        """)
                        for ym in sorted_months[:10]:
                            txns_m = month_map[ym]
                            cnt_m = len(txns_m)
                            disc_m = sum(
                                t.get("total_allowed_discount", 0) or 0 for t in txns_m
                            )
                            exc_m = sum(
                                t.get("total_excess_discount", 0) or 0 for t in txns_m
                            )
                            lbl_m = month_label(ym)
                            ec = "#DC2626" if exc_m > 0 else "#10B981"
                            ui.html(f"""
                            <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 50px 70px 70px;
                                        gap:0;font-size:12px;padding:5px 0;
                                        border-bottom:1px solid #F9FAFB;align-items:center;cursor:pointer"
                                 onclick="location.href='/mis-table?month={ym}'">
                              <span style="font-weight:500;color:#374151">{lbl_m}</span>
                              <span style="text-align:right;font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;color:#6B7280">{cnt_m}</span>
                              <span style="text-align:right;font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;color:#6B7280">₹{disc_m / 1000:.0f}K</span>
                              <span style="text-align:right;font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;color:{ec};font-weight:600">₹{exc_m / 1000:.0f}K</span>
                            </div>
                            """)
                    else:
                        ui.html(
                            '<div style="color:#9CA3AF;font-size:12px;padding:20px 0;text-align:center">No data yet</div>'
                        )


# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
#                   PAGE: MIS TABLE (separate from Dashboard)
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
@ui.page("/mis-table")
async def mis_table_page(month: str | None = None) -> None:
    render_topbar("MIS Table")

    try:
        transactions: list = await api_get("/transactions")
    except Exception:
        transactions = []

    # Filter by month if provided
    if month:
        transactions = [
            t
            for t in transactions
            if (t.get("booking_date", "") or "").startswith(month)
        ]

    total_entries = len(transactions)
    total_excess = sum(t.get("total_excess_discount", 0) or 0 for t in transactions)

    # Month grouping for sidebar
    from collections import defaultdict
    import calendar

    month_map = defaultdict(list)
    for t in await api_get("/transactions") if month else transactions:
        bd = t.get("booking_date", "")
        if bd and len(bd) >= 7:
            month_map[bd[:7]].append(t)
    sorted_months = sorted(month_map.keys(), reverse=True)

    def month_label(ym: str) -> str:
        try:
            y, m = ym.split("-")
            return f"{calendar.month_abbr[int(m)]} {y}"
        except Exception:
            return ym

    with ui.element("div").classes("dash-layout"):
        # ── Sidebar ───────────────────────────────────────────
        with ui.element("div").classes("dash-sidebar"):
            ui.html('<div class="sidebar-section-label">Quick Nav</div>')
            ui.html("""
                <a href="/" class="sidebar-month-item">📊 &nbsp;Dashboard</a>
                <a href="/mis-table" class="sidebar-month-item active">📋 &nbsp;MIS Table</a>
            """)
            ui.html('<div class="sidebar-divider"></div>')
            ui.html('<div class="sidebar-section-label">Month-wise MIS</div>')
            # All months link
            all_active = "" if month else " active"
            ui.html(
                f'<a href="/mis-table" class="sidebar-month-item{all_active}">All Months <span class="sidebar-month-badge">{sum(len(v) for v in month_map.values())}</span></a>'
            )
            for ym in sorted_months:
                cnt = len(month_map[ym])
                exc = sum(1 for t in month_map[ym] if t.get("status") == "Excess")
                lbl = month_label(ym)
                is_active = " active" if month == ym else ""
                badge_style = (
                    ' style="background:#FECDC8;color:#C0392B"' if exc > 0 else ""
                )
                ui.html(
                    f'<a href="/mis-table?month={ym}" class="sidebar-month-item{is_active}">'
                    f'  {lbl} <span class="sidebar-month-badge"{badge_style}>{cnt}</span>'
                    f"</a>"
                )
            ui.html('<div class="sidebar-divider"></div>')
            ui.html("""
                <a href="/form" class="sidebar-month-item">➕ &nbsp;New Entry</a>
                <a href="/settings" class="sidebar-month-item">⚙️ &nbsp;Settings</a>
            """)

        # ── Main ─────────────────────────────────────────────
        with ui.element("div").classes("dash-main"):
            # Header
            title_suffix = f" — {month_label(month)}" if month else " — All Months"
            with ui.element("div").classes("section-header"):
                with ui.element("div"):
                    ui.html(
                        f'<div class="section-title-text">MIS Table{title_suffix}</div>'
                    )
                    exc_badge = (
                        f'<span style="color:#DC2626;font-weight:600"> · ₹{total_excess:,.0f} excess</span>'
                        if total_excess > 0
                        else ""
                    )
                    ui.html(
                        f'<div class="section-subtitle">{total_entries} record{"s" if total_entries != 1 else ""}{exc_badge}</div>'
                    )
                ui.button(
                    "➕  New Entry", on_click=lambda: ui.navigate.to("/form")
                ).classes("btn-add").props("no-caps unelevated")

            with ui.element("div").classes("table-card"):
                render_table(transactions)


# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
#                        PAGE 1: SETTINGS
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════


@ui.page("/settings")
def settings_page():
    render_topbar("Settings")

    with ui.card().classes("page-wrap w-full"):
        ui.label("Upload Price List").classes("text-xl font-bold mb-4")

        # 🔹 Default today
        today = date.today().isoformat()
        with ui.row().classes("justify-end"):
            # 🔹 REQUIRED: valid_from
            valid_from = ui.date_input(
                label="Valid From (Required)", value=today
            ).classes("w-64")

            # 🔹 OPTIONAL: valid_to
            valid_to = ui.date_input(label="Valid To (Optional)").classes("w-64")

            status_label = ui.label("").classes("text-sm mt-2")

            async def handle_upload(e):
                try:
                    if not valid_from.value:
                        status_label.text = "❌ Valid From date is required"
                        status_label.classes("text-red-600")
                        return

                    file = e

                    payload = {
                        # "sheet_name": "0",
                        "valid_from": valid_from.value,
                    }

                    if valid_to.value:
                        payload["valid_to"] = valid_to.value

                    # USE SHARED FILE API
                    await api_post_file("/price-list/upload", file, payload)

                    status_label.text = "✅ Price list uploaded successfully"
                    status_label.classes("text-green-600")

                except Exception as ex:
                    status_label.text = f"❌ {str(ex)}"
                    status_label.classes("text-red-600")

            ui.upload(
                on_upload=handle_upload,
                auto_upload=True,
            ).classes("")

            ui.label("Upload Excel file (.xlsx)").classes("text-xs text-gray-400 mt-2")


# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
#                   PAGE-LOCAL FORM STATE
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
class FormState:
    """
    All mutable state for a single /form session.
    Instantiated inside form_page() — never shared across sessions.
    """

    def __init__(self):
        # Edit mode
        self.txn_id: int | None = None  # set when editing
        self.edit_mode: bool = False

        # Reference data (populated by fetch_reference_data)
        self.cars: list = []
        self.components: list = []
        self.outlets: list = []
        self.executives: list = []

        # Selected foreign keys
        self.car_id: int | None = None
        self.variant_id: int | None = None
        self.outlet_id: int | None = None
        self.executive_id: int | None = None

        # UI element refs — vehicle
        self.car_select: ui.select | None = None
        self.variant_select: ui.select | None = None
        self.booking_date: ui.input | None = None
        self.outlet_select: ui.select | None = None
        self.exec_select: ui.select | None = None
        self.cust_file_no: ui.input | None = None
        self.vin_no: ui.input | None = None
        self.engine_no: ui.input | None = None
        self.model_year: ui.input | None = None
        self.vehicle_regn_no: ui.input | None = None
        self.regn_date: ui.input | None = None

        # UI element refs — customer
        self.cust_name: ui.input | None = None
        self.cust_mobile: ui.input | None = None
        self.cust_email: ui.input | None = None
        self.cust_relative: ui.input | None = None
        self.cust_address: ui.input | None = None
        self.cust_city: ui.input | None = None
        self.cust_pincode: ui.input | None = None
        self.cust_pan: ui.input | None = None
        self.cust_aadhar: ui.input | None = None
        self.cust_other_id: ui.input | None = None

        # UI element refs — accessories / audit
        self.acc_list: ui.textarea | None = None
        self.acc_charged: ui.number | None = None
        self.acc_total_label: ui.label | None = None
        self.acc_select: ui.select | None = None
        self.accessory_allowed: ui.number | None = None
        self.audit_obs: ui.textarea | None = None
        self.audit_action: ui.textarea | None = None
        self.accessory_select: ui.select | None = None
        self.accessory_charged: ui.number | None = None
        self.accessory_total_label: ui.label | None = None

        self.accessory_map: dict = {}  # {id: {name, price}}

        # UI element refs — actions
        self.submit_btn: ui.button | None = None
        self.error_banner: ui.html | None = None

        # Component toggles: to track state of toggle switches
        self.price_match_toggles: dict[str, ui.switch] = {}
        self.discount_match_toggles: dict[str, ui.switch] = {}

        self.listed_prices: dict[str, int] = {}
        self.price_listed_labels: dict[str, ui.label] = {}
        self.discount_listed_labels: dict[str, ui.label] = {}

        # Component inputs: name → ui.number
        self.price_inputs: dict[str, ui.number] = {}
        self.discount_inputs: dict[str, ui.number] = {}

        # Checkboxes
        self.condition_cbs: dict[str, ui.checkbox] = {}
        self.delivery_cbs: dict[str, ui.checkbox] = {}

        # Invoice Section
        self.invoice_number: ui.input | None = None
        self.invoice_date: ui.input | None = None
        self.invoice_ex_showroom: ui.number | None = None
        self.invoice_discount: ui.number | None = None
        self.invoice_taxable_value: ui.number | None = None
        self.invoice_cgst: ui.number | None = None
        self.invoice_sgst: ui.number | None = None
        self.invoice_igst: ui.number | None = None
        self.invoice_cess: ui.number | None = None
        self.invoice_total: ui.number | None = None

        # Payment Section
        self.payment_cash: ui.number | None = None
        self.payment_bank: ui.number | None = None
        self.payment_finance: ui.number | None = None
        self.payment_exchange: ui.number | None = None

        # Live calc labels
        self.lbl_discount: ui.label | None = None
        self.lbl_excess: ui.label | None = None

    # ── computed ─────────────────────────────────────────
    @property
    def all_component_inputs(self) -> dict[str, ui.number]:
        return {**self.price_inputs, **self.discount_inputs}

    @property
    def live_discount(self) -> int:
        return sum(int(inp.value or 0) for inp in self.discount_inputs.values())

    def is_valid(self) -> tuple[bool, str]:
        def _val(f):
            return (f.value or "").strip() if f else ""

        def _val_upper(f):
            return (f.value or "").strip().upper() if f else ""

        if not self.variant_id:
            return False, "Please select a Car and Variant."

        name = _val(self.cust_name)
        if not name:
            return False, "Customer name is required."

        mob = _val(self.cust_mobile)
        if not re.fullmatch(r"[6-9]\d{9}", mob):
            return False, "Mobile must be 10 digits starting with 6–9."

        if not _val(self.cust_address):
            return False, "Address is required."

        if not _val(self.cust_city):
            return False, "City is required."

        # if not re.fullmatch(r"\d{6}", _val(self.cust_pincode)):
        #     return False, "Valid 6-digit PIN code required."

        if not re.fullmatch(r"[A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z]", _val_upper(self.cust_pan)):
            return False, "Valid PAN required."

        # if not re.fullmatch(r"\d{12}", _val(self.cust_aadhar)):
        #     return False, "Valid Aadhar required."

        # TR Case condition
        if self.condition_cbs.get("tr_case") and self.condition_cbs["tr_case"].value:
            if not _val(self.cust_other_id):
                return False, "Other ID Proof required for TR Case."

        if not _val(self.cust_file_no):
            return False, "Customer File Number is required."

        if not _val(self.vin_no):
            return False, "VIN Number is required."

        if not _val(self.engine_no):
            return False, "Engine Number is required."

        year = _val(self.model_year)
        if not year or not str(year).isdigit():
            return False, "Valid Model Year is required."

        return True, ""


# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# FORM SECTION BUILDERS
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
def build_form_sec_vehicle(state: FormState) -> None:
    car_opts = {car["id"]: car["name"] for car in state.cars}
    outlet_opts = {outlet["id"]: outlet["name"] for outlet in state.outlets}
    exec_opts = {executive["id"]: executive["name"] for executive in state.executives}

    with ui.element("div").classes("fs-card"):
        ui.html('<div class="fs-title">🚙 &nbsp;Vehicle &amp; Delivery Details</div>')
        with ui.grid(columns=5).classes("w-full gap-2"):
            state.car_select = (
                ui.select(
                    options=car_opts,
                    label="Car *",
                    with_input=True,
                    on_change=lambda e: _fs_on_car_change(e.value, state),
                )
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
            )
            state.variant_select = (
                ui.select(
                    options={},
                    with_input=True,
                    label="Variant *",
                    on_change=lambda e: _fs_on_variant_change(e.value, state),
                )
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
                .on("update:model-value", lambda _: _fs_revalidate(state))
            )
            state.booking_date = (
                ui.input(
                    label="Booking Date *",
                    value=str(date.today()),
                    on_change=lambda _: _fs_try_price_preload(state),
                )
                .classes("w-full")
                .props('type="date" outlined dense')
                .on("update:model-value", lambda _: _fs_revalidate(state))
            )
            # TODO: Get outlet from user profile once auth is implemented, and make this non-editable for most users
            state.outlet_select = (
                ui.select(
                    options=outlet_opts,
                    label="Outlet",
                    on_change=lambda e: setattr(state, "outlet_id", e.value),
                )
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
            )
            state.exec_select = (
                ui.select(
                    options=exec_opts,
                    label="Sales Executive",
                    on_change=lambda e: setattr(state, "executive_id", e.value),
                )
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
            )

            state.cust_file_no = (
                ui.input(label="Customer File No *")
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
                .on("update:model-value", lambda _: _fs_revalidate(state))
            )

            state.vin_no = (
                ui.input(label="VIN Number *")
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
                .on("update:model-value", lambda _: _fs_revalidate(state))
            )

            state.engine_no = (
                ui.input(label="Engine Number *")
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
                .on("update:model-value", lambda _: _fs_revalidate(state))
            )

            state.model_year = (
                ui.input(label="Model Year *", placeholder="e.g. 2024")
                .classes("w-full")
                .props('outlined dense type="number"')
                .on("update:model-value", lambda _: _fs_revalidate(state))
            )
            state.vehicle_regn_no = (
                ui.input(label="Vehicle Regn Number")
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
            )

            state.regn_date = (
                ui.input(label="Date of Registration")
                .classes("w-full")
                .props('outlined dense type="date"')
            )
        # Set defaults for outlet / exec
        if state.outlets:
            state.outlet_select.set_value(state.outlets[0]["id"])
            state.outlet_id = state.outlets[0]["id"]
        if state.executives:
            state.exec_select.set_value(state.executives[0]["id"])
            state.executive_id = state.executives[0]["id"]


# def build_form_sec_customer(state: FormState) -> None:
#     with ui.element("div").classes("fs-card"):
#         ui.html('<div class="fs-title">👤 &nbsp;Customer</div>')
#         with ui.grid(columns=3).classes("w-full gap-2"):
#             state.cust_name = (
#                 ui.input(label="Name *", placeholder="Full name")
#                 .classes("w-full")
#                 .props("outlined dense")
#                 .on("blur", lambda: _fs_revalidate(state))
#             )
#             state.cust_mobile = (
#                 ui.input(label="Mobile *", placeholder="10-digit")
#                 .classes("w-full")
#                 .props("outlined dense")
#                 .on("blur", lambda: _fs_validate_mobile(state))
#             )
#             state.cust_email = (
#                 ui.input(label="Email", placeholder="optional")
#                 .classes("w-full")
#                 .props("outlined dense")
#             )
def build_form_sec_customer(state: FormState) -> None:
    with ui.element("div").classes("fs-card"):
        ui.html('<div class="fs-title">👤 &nbsp;Customer</div>')

        # ── Basic Info ─────────────────────────────
        with ui.grid(columns=3).classes("w-full gap-2"):
            state.cust_name = (
                ui.input(label="Name *", placeholder="Full name")
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
                .on("update:model-value", lambda _: _fs_revalidate(state))
            )
            state.cust_mobile = (
                ui.input(
                    label="Mobile *",
                    placeholder="10-digit",
                    validation={
                        "Must be 10 digits starting 6–9": lambda v: (
                            not v or re.fullmatch(r"[6-9]\d{9}", v)
                        )
                    },
                )
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
                .on("update:model-value", lambda _: _fs_validate_mobile(state))
            )
            state.cust_email = (
                ui.input(label="Email", placeholder="optional")
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
            )

            state.cust_relative = (
                ui.input(label="Relative Name", placeholder="optional")
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
            )

            state.cust_address = (
                ui.input(label="Address *")
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
                .on("update:model-value", lambda _: _fs_revalidate(state))
            )

            state.cust_city = (
                ui.input(label="City *")
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
                .on("update:model-value", lambda _: _fs_revalidate(state))
            )

            state.cust_pincode = (
                ui.input(
                    label="Pin Code *",
                    placeholder="6 digits",
                    validation={
                        "Must be 6 digits": lambda v: (
                            len(re.sub(r"\D", "", v or "")) == 6
                        )
                    },
                )
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
                .on("update:model-value", lambda _: _fs_validate_pincode(state))
            )

            state.cust_pan = (
                ui.input(
                    label="PAN *",
                    placeholder="ABCDE1234F",
                    validation={
                        "Invalid PAN Format": lambda v: (
                            not v or re.fullmatch(r"[A-Z]{5}[0-9]{4}[A-Z]", v.upper())
                        )
                    },
                )
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
                .on(
                    "update:model-value",
                    lambda e: (
                        state.cust_pan.set_value(e.value.upper()),
                        _fs_validate_pan(state),
                    ),
                )
            )

            state.cust_aadhar = (
                ui.input(
                    label="Aadhar *",
                    placeholder="12 digits",
                    validation={
                        "Must be 12 digits": lambda v: (
                            len(re.sub(r"\D", "", v or "")) == 12
                        )
                    },
                )
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
                .on("update:model-value", lambda _: _fs_validate_aadhar(state))
            )

            # ── Conditional Field (TR Case) ────────────
            state.cust_other_id = (
                ui.input(label="Other ID Proof")
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense")
            )


def build_form_sec_conditions(state: FormState) -> None:
    with ui.element("div").classes("fs-card"):
        ui.html('<div class="fs-title">☑️ &nbsp;Sale Conditions</div>')
        with ui.row().classes("flex-wrap gap-4"):
            for key, label in CONDITION_KEYS:
                state.condition_cbs[key] = (
                    ui.checkbox(label)
                    .props("dense")
                    .on("update:model-value", lambda _: _fs_revalidate(state))
                )


def build_form_sec_prices(state: FormState) -> None:
    price_comps = sorted(
        [
            price_comp
            for price_comp in state.components
            if price_comp.get("type") == "price"
        ],
        key=lambda x: x.get("order", 99),
    )
    discount_comps = sorted(
        [
            discount_comp
            for discount_comp in state.components
            if discount_comp.get("type") == "discount"
        ],
        key=lambda x: x.get("order", 99),
    )

    with ui.element("div").classes("fs-card"):
        ui.html('<div class="fs-title">💰 &nbsp;Price &amp; Discounts</div>')

        ui.html('<div class="fs-subtitle">Price Charged</div>')
        if price_comps:
            with ui.grid(columns=1).classes("w-full gap-2"):
                for comp in price_comps:
                    name = comp["name"]

                    with ui.row().classes("w-full items-center gap-2"):
                        # Label
                        ui.label(name).classes("w-40 text-xs")

                        # Listed price display
                        listed_label = ui.label("₹—").classes(
                            "w-32 text-gray-500 text-xs"
                        )
                        state.price_listed_labels[name] = listed_label

                        # Toggle (Match Listed Price)
                        toggle = (
                            ui.switch("Match Listed Price")
                            .classes("m-10")
                            .props('dense icon="check" color="green"')
                        )

                        # Input
                        inp = (
                            ui.number(
                                placeholder="Enter Charged Price", format="%.0f", min=0
                            )
                            .classes("w-60 num-input")
                            .props("outlined dense")
                        )

                        state.price_inputs[name] = inp
                        state.price_match_toggles[name] = toggle

                        # def on_toggle(e, name=name, inp=inp):
                        #     if e.args:
                        #         # copy listed price
                        #         val = state.listed_prices.get(name, 0)
                        #         inp.set_value(val)
                        #         inp.props("readonly")
                        #     else:
                        #         inp.set_value(None)
                        #         inp.props("remove=disable")

                        def on_toggle(_, name=name, inp=inp, toggle=toggle):
                            if toggle.value:
                                val = state.listed_prices.get(name, 0)
                                inp.set_value(val)
                                inp.set_enabled(False)  # ✅ disable input
                            else:
                                inp.set_enabled(True)  # ✅ re-enable input
                                inp.set_value(None)  # optional: clear

                        toggle.on("update:model-value", on_toggle)

        else:
            ui.label("No price components — check /components endpoint.").classes(
                "text-xs text-gray-400"
            )

        ui.html(
            '<div class="fs-subtitle" style="margin-top:12px">Discounts Offered</div>'
        )
        if discount_comps:
            with ui.grid(columns=1).classes("w-full gap-2"):
                for comp in discount_comps:
                    name = comp["name"]

                    with ui.row().classes("w-full items-center gap-2"):
                        ui.label(name).classes("w-40 text-xs")

                        listed_label = ui.label("₹—").classes(
                            "w-32 text-gray-500 text-xs"
                        )
                        state.discount_listed_labels[name] = listed_label

                        toggle = (
                            ui.switch("Standard Discount")
                            .props("dense icon=check color=green")
                            .classes("m-10")
                        )

                        inp = (
                            ui.number(placeholder="₹", format="%.0f", min=0)
                            .classes("w-60 num-input")
                            .props("outlined dense")
                            .on("update:model-value", lambda: _fs_update_live(state))
                        )

                        state.discount_inputs[name] = inp
                        state.discount_match_toggles[name] = toggle

                        def on_toggle(_, name=name, inp=inp, toggle=toggle):
                            if toggle.value:
                                val = state.listed_prices.get(name, 0)
                                inp.set_value(val)
                                inp.set_enabled(False)  # ✅ disable input
                            else:
                                inp.set_enabled(True)  # ✅ re-enable input
                                inp.set_value(None)  # optional: clear

                        toggle.on("update:model-value", on_toggle)

        else:
            ui.label("No discount components — check /components endpoint.").classes(
                "text-xs text-gray-400"
            )


def build_form_sec_accessories(state: FormState) -> None:
    with ui.element("div").classes("fs-card"):
        ui.html('<div class="fs-title">🔧 &nbsp;Accessories</div>')

        # Placeholder options (replace with dynamic from state.accessory_map)
        # state.accessory_map = {
        #     1: {"name": "Floor Mats", "price": 2000},
        #     2: {"name": "Seat Covers", "price": 5000},
        #     3: {"name": "Car Cover", "price": 3000},
        #     4: {"name": "Roof Rack", "price": 4500},
        # }

        options = {
            acc_id: f"{data['name']} (₹{data['price']})"
            for acc_id, data in state.accessory_map.items()
        }

        def update_total(e):
            selected = e.value or []
            total = sum(
                state.accessory_map[int(i)]["price"]
                for i in selected
                if int(i) in state.accessory_map
            )

            state.acc_total_label.set_text(f"₹{total:,.0f}")

            # auto-fill charged if empty
            if not state.acc_charged.value:
                state.acc_charged.set_value(total)

        # ── Multi-select ───────────────────────────
        with ui.grid(columns=3).classes("items-center gap-4"):
            state.acc_select = (
                ui.select(
                    options=options,
                    label="Select Accessories",
                    multiple=True,
                    with_input=True,  # search enabled
                    on_change=update_total,
                )
                .classes("w-full")
                .props("outlined dense use-input")
            )

            # ── Total Display ──────────────────────────
            state.acc_total_label = ui.label("₹0").classes("text-sm text-gray-600")

            # ── Charged Input ─────────────────────────
            state.acc_charged = (
                ui.number(label="Actual Charged (₹)", format="%.0f", min=0)
                .classes("w-full num-input")
                .props("outlined dense")
            )

            )


def build_form_sec_invoice(state: FormState) -> None:
    def calculate_taxes():
        taxable = state.invoice_taxable_value.value or 0

        # # derive rate dynamically if existing values present
        # cgst_rate = (state.invoice_cgst.value or 0) / taxable if taxable else 0
        # sgst_rate = (state.invoice_sgst.value or 0) / taxable if taxable else 0

        cgst = taxable * 0.09
        sgst = taxable * 0.09

        state.invoice_cgst.set_value(int(cgst))
        state.invoice_sgst.set_value(int(sgst))
        calculate_total()

    def calculate_total():
        taxable = state.invoice_taxable_value.value or 0
        cgst = state.invoice_cgst.value or 0
        sgst = state.invoice_sgst.value or 0
        igst = state.invoice_igst.value or 0 if state.igst_toggle.value else 0
        cess = state.invoice_cess.value or 0 if state.cess_toggle.value else 0

        total = taxable + cgst + sgst + igst + cess
        state.invoice_total.set_value(int(total))

    # Removed premature call here to avoid AttributeError

    with ui.element("div").classes("fs-card"):
        ui.html('<div class="fs-title">🧾 &nbsp;Invoice Details</div>')

        with ui.grid(columns=3).classes("w-full gap-2"):
            state.invoice_number = ui.input(label="Invoice Number").props(
                "outlined dense"
            )
            state.invoice_date = ui.input(label="Invoice Date").props(
                'outlined dense type="date"'
            )

            state.invoice_ex_showroom = ui.number(
                label="Ex-Showroom Price (Synced)", format="%.0f"
            ).props("outlined dense readonly")
            state.invoice_ex_showroom.on(
                "update:model-value", lambda: _fs_update_live(state)
            )

            state.invoice_discount = ui.number(label="Discount", format="%.0f").props(
                "outlined dense"
            )
            state.invoice_discount.on(
                "update:model-value", lambda: _fs_update_live(state)
            )
            state.invoice_taxable_value = ui.number(
                label="Taxable Value", format="%.0f"
            ).props("outlined dense")

            state.invoice_taxable_value.on(
                "update:model-value",
                lambda _: (
                    calculate_taxes(),
                    calculate_total(),
                    _fs_update_live(state),
                ),
            )

            state.invoice_cgst = ui.number(label="CGST", format="%.0f").props(
                "outlined dense"
            )
            state.invoice_cgst.on("update:model-value", calculate_total)

            state.invoice_sgst = ui.number(label="SGST", format="%.0f").props(
                "outlined dense"
            )
            state.invoice_sgst.on("update:model-value", calculate_total)

            state.igst_toggle = ui.switch("Apply IGST").props("dense")
            state.invoice_igst = ui.number(label="IGST", format="%.0f").props(
                "outlined dense"
            )
            state.invoice_igst.on("update:model-value", calculate_total)

            state.cess_toggle = ui.switch("Apply CESS").props("dense")
            state.invoice_cess = ui.number(label="CESS", format="%.0f").props(
                "outlined dense"
            )
            state.invoice_cess.on("update:model-value", calculate_total)

            state.invoice_total = ui.number(
                label="Total Invoice Value", format="%.0f"
            ).props("outlined dense")

        def toggle_taxes():
            state.invoice_igst.set_enabled(state.igst_toggle.value)
            state.invoice_cess.set_enabled(state.cess_toggle.value)

        state.igst_toggle.on(
            "update:model-value", lambda _: (toggle_taxes(), calculate_total())
        )
        state.cess_toggle.on(
            "update:model-value", lambda _: (toggle_taxes(), calculate_total())
        )
        toggle_taxes()
        calculate_total()
